[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDuring a fuzzing session of the `ExpanderFuzzer` harness against the Apache Commons[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCompress library, the fuzzer triggered a Java heap exhaustion. The crash is [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mclassified as a low‐severity security issue [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueLow`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanifests as a `java.lang.OutOfMemoryError` in the LZW decompression code path when[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprocessing a malformed or adversarial input.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  While running the `ExpanderFuzzer` with Jazzer and libFuzzer instrumentation, the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtarget application attempted to decompress the provided test case. During [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitialization of the LZW decoding tables inside [0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.lzw.LZWInputStream.initializeTables`, the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mJava VM ran out of heap memory and threw an `OutOfMemoryError`. Jazzer reported [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthis as a low‐severity security finding [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`FuzzerSecurityIssueLow: Out of memory`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Vulnerability Type  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The issue is reported under the typical category of “Out of Memory” failures in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfuzzing, indicating unbounded or excessive memory allocation in response to crafted[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minputs. No other vulnerability class [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., buffer overflow, injection[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmentioned.[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Key Observations  [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The crash occurs in the LZW decompression implementation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m186[0m[39m & [0m[1;36m220[0m[39m of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`LZWInputStream.java`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The stack trace ascends through the Z format decompressor [0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`ZCompressorInputStream`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, the compressor factory [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39m`CompressorStreamFactory.createCompressorInputStream`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, and the example expander [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcode [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`Expander.decompress` → `Expander.expand`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • Jazzer instruments large portions of both Commons Compress and Commons IO, but [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe failure is localized to the decompression logic.  [0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The fuzzer ran with a limited timeout and memory limit but still exhausted the [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mheap, indicating that the code under test does not bound resource usage based on [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minput.[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Code Areas for Investigation  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  To fully understand the root cause and the memory growth profile, the following [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcomponents should be reviewed:  [0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.lzw.LZWInputStream` – table [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minitialization and growth strategy.  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. `org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.z.ZCompressorInputStream` – [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mintegration of LZW logic.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. `org.apache.commons.compress.compressors.CompressorStreamFactory` – how it [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mselects and configures the decompression stream.  [0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. `org.apache.commons.compress.archivers.examples.Expander` – the example entry [0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Fuzzer harness [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`ExpanderFuzzer.fuzzerTestOneInput`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m – to confirm it simply [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpasses raw bytes into the expander without internal protections.[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNo speculation on the underlying cause or remediation strategies is included; the [0m  [2m                [0m
